			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				name = "Deutsche Kolonialgesellschaft"
				long_name = "Deutsche Kolonialgesellschaft"
			}

			GER = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = TUN
					autonomous_state = kx_colored_puppet
				}
			}

			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
	}
}
